Education News

Ministry of Education Explains the Distinction Between Elementary School Names 216

The Ministry of Education, based on a submission from the Anhui Education Department regarding Article 11 of the elementary school regulations promulgated by the Ministry, which stipulates that provincial elementary schools shall be named after the place where they are located, and public elementary schools below the county and city level shall use place names of smaller areas as school names. When there are two or more identical public elementary schools in one place, they may be distinguished by the order of numbers. According to this, provincial elementary schools in the same location should be distinguished by First and Second, such as Anhui Provincial Anqing First Elementary School, Anhui Provincial Anqing Second Elementary School, etc. County elementary schools in the same county seat can also be named such as XX County City First Elementary School, XX County City Second Elementary School, etc. It is investigated that the elementary schools in the provincial capital of this province are all provincial. Can the above names be used to correct the current names, or should they be renamed Anhui Provincial Anqing XX (street name or lane name) Elementary School? Can the county elementary schools in each county seat be distinguished by numbers, or should they be renamed XX County, XX (street name or lane name) Elementary School? The Department did not dare to make a decision on its own, and therefore presents this request for examination and instructions to follow. The Department was instructed: It is investigated that the elementary schools in the provincial capital and various other levels of

elementary schools in county districts can be named after street and lane names, but if there are two or more identical elementary schools established on the same street or lane, they can be distinguished by numbers. You are to be informed immediately.

Results of the Fourth Shandong Provincial Middle School Graduation Examination Announced ▲ 1,575 Pass, Marked Improvement Over Previous Years ▲ Students Are All Working Hard Towards Practical Science 丨 First Place Awarded Xu Xinglin a Book Coupon Worth 100 Yuan 丨 High School Students with 85 Points Exempted from Entrance Examination 217

(Jinan Correspondence) The fourth provincial middle school graduation examination in this province was held in twenty-one districts throughout the province, starting on the 26th of last month and ending on the 28th. Due to continuous rain and muddy roads, the examination papers from various districts arrived in Jinan late. The members of the Examination Committee, despite the sweltering heat, reviewed the examination papers and calculated the scores late into the night. It is now completed and was announced on the 16th. It is calculated that this time, including those who participated in the examination and those who took the makeup exam from the previous session, there were more than 3,200 people in total. 1,575 passed. Calculated as a percentage, about 77% passed, 16% failed two or more subjects and should take a makeup exam, and 7% failed three or more subjects and should repeat the grade. The number is less than the previous session. The middle schools that previously had poorer performance have also shown great improvement. In Anqiu, Changqing, Dongping and other county middle schools, not a single student repeated the grade. There were three students with scores above 90 in the first session, three in the second and third sessions, and this session suddenly increased to seven. This is with the examination scores and school scores calculated together. If the examination scores were calculated separately, there would be even more students with scores above 90. This shows that students are all diligently studying. The Education Department intends to give the best students prizes in addition to exempting them from the entrance examination to encourage them. The specific method has not yet been determined. In terms of subjects, Chinese and Party Principles were better in the previous sessions, while science was inferior, with biology being the worst. Although Chinese and Party Principles were not as good as before in this session, science has greatly improved. It can be seen that students are all working hard towards practical science. This new change is quite noteworthy. All of the above proves that the previous examinations have had a very significant effect.

(Jinan, 17th) The school performance in the middle school examination is as follows: Grade A (80 points or above): Jinan First Junior Middle School; Grade B (70 points or above): Dexian Provincial Junior Middle School and 13 other schools; Grade C (60 points or above): Zhucheng Provincial Junior Middle School and 31 other schools; Grade D (50 points or above): Jinan Private Zhengyi Junior Middle School and 3 other schools. In terms of student performance, Xu Xinglin of Jinan Girls' Middle School scored 95 points, the highest in the province, and was awarded a book coupon worth 100 yuan. The remaining six students with scores above 90 were awarded 80 yuan in book coupons for second place, 60 yuan for third place, and 50 yuan each for fourth to seventh place. A total of 78 students with scores above 85 were exempted from the written entrance examination. In addition, six high school students with scores above 85 were exempted from the written entrance examination. The Education Department awarded book coupons worth 100 yuan, 80 yuan, and 60 yuan to the first, second, and third place students at Shandong University, Shandong Provincial Medical College, and Qilu University, respectively.

Educational Research Institute of the National Central University to Recruit Graduate Students 221

The College of Education of the National Central University is the earliest established and most prestigious academic research and talent cultivation institution in education in the country. In the past twenty years, almost all activities that have promoted the cause of education have been closely related to the College. The College has conducted many experimental studies over the years. In February of this year, it also established an Educational Research Institute, concentrating talent and equipment, expanding the scope of experiments, and making more important contributions to the solution of current educational problems in our country. The founding process and general situation of the Institute have been reported in previous newspapers. Now, it is heard that in response to requests from various parties, it has been decided to recruit eight graduate students during this summer vacation to engage in various experimental studies under the guidance of professors. Graduates from education or psychology departments of domestic universities, or graduates from other departments with education or psychology as a minor, are eligible to apply. The recruitment brochure will be announced soon. The current talent and equipment of the Institute and the treatment of graduate students are excerpted below:

(1) Talents: All professors from the Education and Psychology departments of the National Central University are instructors at the Institute. The two departments currently have eighteen professors, all of whom are the most renowned educational scholars and psychologists in the country, such as Ai Xianzhou, Du Zuozhou, Xiao Xiaorong, Xu Kesheng, Zhang Shiyi, Meng Xiancheng, Chen Jianxiu, Pan Huo, Wu Nanxuan, Wang Shulin, Gao Junshan, Zhao Gengchuan, Zhong Daozan, Gui Zhibai, Xiong Wenmin, Wang Fengming, Xia Chengfeng, and Zhao Tingwei. The abundance of talent is unprecedented.

(2) Equipment: All equipment from the Education and Psychology departments of the National Central University is available for use by graduate students of the Institute. The two departments currently have 5,000 specialized books and 800 kinds of magazines. There is a library and a research room, each very spacious and capable of accommodating more than 100 people for research work. In addition, the Institute has obtained 452 sets of textbooks from major bookstores at home and abroad. In the future, it will continue to collect or purchase other educational materials. Once the Institute's specialized buildings are completed, rooms will be set up for display. Regarding psychological instruments and experimental supplies, there are currently more than 2,300 pieces, worth nearly 40,000 yuan, divided into two major categories: general psychological instruments and testing and statistical instruments. Newly purchased industrial psychology instruments and computers have been shipped. There are still many varieties that have been ordered but not yet received. Recently, the German Consulate in Nanjing has expressed its willingness to collect a large number of psychological instruments, books, children's toys, and other educational materials from Germany for the Institute to display. The above equipment will be supplied to graduate students as much as possible in the future.

(3) Treatment of Graduate Students: The Institute offers generous treatment to the graduate students it plans to recruit. The important items include three aspects: (A) An annual stipend of 360 to 420 yuan will be given, and the amount will be distributed monthly once it is determined. (B) In addition to exemption from tuition and miscellaneous fees, books, instruments, and materials will be provided free of charge. (C) Graduate students may take one or two courses at the College.

The application period for graduate students at the Institute has been set from now until the end of July. The examination period is on August 21st and 22nd. For detailed information, please contact the Institute for a brochure.

Order from the Municipal Education Bureau Regarding the Method of Calculating Military Training Grades for High Schools and Above 223

Yesterday, the Municipal Education Bureau instructed private high schools and above in the city, stating: "In the case of Instruction No. 8121 from the Ministry of Education, it is stated that, as approved by the Training Directorate, the method of calculating military training grades for students in high schools and above has been previously agreed upon and implemented. Now, it has been found that some students in various schools do have diseases that prevent them from engaging in strenuous exercise, and the calculation of their scores for those who have been approved to be exempted from practical training should be specified so that various schools can follow. The Ministry now intends to stipulate that, for students who have been approved to be exempted from military training practical training, the score for military training academics will be used as their military training grade. We hereby consult to check if you agree and hope that your Ministry will issue an order to your subordinates to comply with this, and we look forward to a reply, etc." In addition to replying in agreement and issuing separate orders, we hereby urgently order you to inform all public and private high schools and above under your jurisdiction to comply with this order, etc. We hereby order you to comply with this order."

High School Graduates from Unregistered Schools May Still Take Entrance Exams First ▲Then Take a Supplementary Pre-Entrance Exam 224

According to the regulations of the Ministry of Education, graduates from unregistered private high schools are not allowed to take entrance exams for registered universities. However, in order to remedy the situation for graduates from unregistered middle schools and allow them to continue their studies without wasting their education, the Municipal Education Bureau held a pre-entrance exam last year. Those who passed the pre-entrance exam were qualified to take entrance exams for registered universities. Now, it has been found that there are many graduates from unregistered private middle schools in the city in the second semester of the 22nd year. The question of whether they can take entrance exams for registered universities has attracted the attention of school authorities. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency went to the Municipal Education Bureau to inquire about the truth. According to Commissioner Zhou Shang of the Bureau, the graduates of unregistered high schools this year will still take the entrance exams first according to last year's method before the Ministry of Education determines a method. After the method is determined, they will take a supplementary pre-entrance exam.

New Tennis Techniques (8) by J. PARMLY PARET, Translated by Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun 丨Copyright Reserved, Reproduction Prohibited丨 247

Furthermore, if the player does not make the most of the follow-through, then the power of the stroke will inevitably be slowed down invisibly. Therefore, one must avoid loosening the force unless the racket follows the arm to use up all the power before stopping. To do this, one must make the racket light and flexible when swinging, which requires making full use of the follow-through. Furthermore, the racket following the arm to exhaust the power can also automatically affect the spin of the hit ball. The effect of this type of ball spin will be studied in detail later when discussing hitting techniques and the effect of ball spin.

(Note) This paragraph should be connected to the end of Chapter 2, that is, the last section of (6) published on the 16th. The following is connected to (7) published on the next 7th (that is, Chapter 3, Serving)

When serving, tennis players use different hitting methods, but in any case, the most common method is to turn the arm behind the head before actually hitting, and the wrist folds the racket, so that the racket head faces backward. Some players only lower the racket head to the same level as the wrist, and some players lower the racket head below the shoulder or rest it on the shoulder. When the racket head is down, the wrist is bent backward. When hitting, the force that splits forward from the shoulder to the upper arm to the lower arm will drag the wrist and racket forward. However, at this time, the racket is still hanging behind the wrist. When hitting the ball, the wrist will immediately fold the racket forward again, the racket will be straightened, and the ball will be heavily split.

When serving, the ball must be turned downwards and obliquely. It is actually impossible to serve over the head without twisting the ball downwards. Because when hitting, if you only erect the racket and shoot the ball straight to the opponent, as long as the speed of the ball is slightly stronger, it will inevitably cross the boundary. From this point of view, twisting the ball can not only guide the flight of the ball, but also

make the ball just fall within the boundary of the opponent's service area.

The method of twisting the ball will be studied in detail later. Now we only need to know that twisting the ball is to make the flight of the ball oblique, not flying straight out. If the player twists the ball from the side, the ball will slightly twist its direction and fly away because it touches the side of the racket. Therefore, when hitting the ball, the racket head turns forward and pounces, which will cause the ball to tend to twist, causing it to fall slightly downwards out of a straight line. The greater the twisting force, the heavier the hitting force must be, and it can also make the ball accurately fall

within the opponent's very narrow service area.

Based on the above principles, Americans have invented a twisting serve, and it has proven to be very effective. This method hits the ball with great force, and at the same time adds a great twisting force on the side of the ball, so the ball quickly rotates towards the opponent, and lands extremely quickly, and then emits an extremely unpredictable rebound from the ground. To produce this effect, the server's body must first lean back, and then straighten up smoothly. When the ball is in contact with the ball, the hitting action is upward and outward.

The most difficult part of this American twisting serve is to make the ball and the racket have a long contact time within the possible range, so that the ball can rotate once on the racket surface, so that the ball has an extremely fast rotation force when it flies out. The initial contact point between the racket and the ball is at the lower rear of the ball, and then it takes advantage of the trend to turn upwards and outwards to the right. When the ball is about to be hit, the racket head must also contact the top of the ball, so that it flies obliquely to the ground to the opponent, and generates extremely fast rotation force. This American serve is very difficult to learn. Beginners should not try it lightly before they have mastered the ordinary overhead straight shot.

Since the basic work of serving is to make the ball fly over the net and just fall within the restricted area, it is not easy for beginners to succeed without hard practice. When practicing, it is best to ask a friend to stand on the other side so that the ball can be thrown back, so that the ball can be served to the opponent again and again, until it can achieve the purpose every time, that is considered the beginning of success in ball skills.

Furthermore, the technique should be practiced faster and faster, until the ball flies out with absolute accuracy. If the ball is shot straight to the opponent, and the landing point is always accurately over the boundary of the service area by several feet, then the beginner must not be discouraged at this time, but should add more effort, then the flight of the ball can be easily shortened, and the movement of hitting the ball is still very fast, then you have to use the above-mentioned twisting hitting method. Because the ball is forced by a very heavy twisting force, it will certainly not still form a straight line when it flies out, and its flight will also be shortened.

The actual action of serving is to use the tendency of the arm to pounce forward, and the wrist takes advantage of the trend to twist the backward racket over, and then use the force from the shoulder and arm to quickly sweep the ball forward. At this time, the extremely fast momentum of the racket, plus the body weight and the rotation of the shoulder, makes the force of shooting the ball extremely large.

When the serving action reaches the final stage when the ball is about to leave the racket, the arm should follow the trend and pounce the racket downwards as much as possible, just like returning the ball in the court as usual, and naturally stop only after exhausting the follow-through force. The actions of some famous tennis players after hitting the ball are different. Some rackets must pounce downwards as much as possible, and the racket head reaches the left or right of the left foot, or just in front of the left foot. As for the American twisting serve, because the racket is pouncing to the side, the racket head is always dragged to the right side of the player's body when it falls. Some players who are good at using the twisting method only have the racket head falling on the right side of the right knee, and there are one or two players whose racket drop is higher than this, even just outside the right side.

A missed serve can be said to be "over" the first time, and "fault" the second time, so after one mistake, you must concentrate and never let it repeat the same mistake, thus losing a point. Experienced players never make mistakes due to negligence when serving. When serving, never use force, the more you force, the easier it is to make mistakes, so you should practice often, so that the hitting technique is extremely free, light and easy, with a calm attitude, and the ball is shot accurately at the prepared position, even if there is a mistake, you can still be calm, that is considered to be deeply aware of the

essence of ball skills.

Since the privilege of serving is at hand, it is necessary to make the best use of it, and never let this attack weapon be as if it does not exist.

Spring and Autumn

Royal Incense Floating Record 248

— Original work by Princess Deling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

Among the many people I have seen in my life, he can be considered the most unfortunate character! At the same time, he is also the most lovable person.

I think this trip to Fengtian will at least give him some comfort!

(10) (1) Female officials and palace maids

This time, the Empress Dowager went to Fengtian. Due to the limited capacity of the carriages, all the arrangements were greatly reduced. She could not bring too many female officials and palace maids who served her closely. In addition to the eight of us female officials who followed her, she only brought sixteen palace maids. These people did not receive any salary and were considered volunteer positions. The origins of us female officials were almost all daughters of high-ranking Manchu officials. The palace maids were selected from the most beautiful daughters of many Manchu soldiers and generals. In name, female officials were certainly nobler than palace maids, but in practice, I believe

that in many ways, it was more comfortable to be a palace maid than a female official.

Being a female official in the Qing Palace not only did not receive a salary, but was also a bitter job that had to be paid for. To be honest, when my sister and I were in the palace, my father often had to send money in for us to use. Every month, Rong Ling and I spent a full one hundred taels of silver just to reward those cooks. The Empress Dowager would also give us things from time to time, which cost even more. Because when the Empress Dowager gave us things, she had to teach the eunuchs to hold them and send them over, and these eunuchs had to be given tips. Moreover, they all had a mind full of commercialized ideas. For example, if the Empress Dowager gave us six or seven things at a time, they would each take one and send them over six or seven times. By doing this, our money was spent even more easily. For example, if six or seven things were sent at once, we only needed to give them twenty or thirty taels of silver for tips. If they were divided into six or seven times, we would have to give at least ten taels each time, which would add up to sixty or seventy taels. (85)

An Old Woman in Qingjiangpu 249

— Wang Shouqiu

In a certain year, something like this happened in Qingjiangpu: When the XXX army attacked Qingjiangpu, there was not even a single soldier in Qingjiangpu city. The XXX army, which was accustomed to killing and arson, had already reached five or six li away from the South Gate and was about to enter the city. If they entered the city of Qingjiangpu, the place would definitely be ruined. But at this time, the people of Qingjiangpu were all hiding in their homes, and there was not a single person on the street. How could they stop this team of robber soldiers? At this critical moment, a very dangerous moment, an old woman suddenly appeared. She could not bear to see such a large Qingjiangpu being raped and looted by these robber soldiers, so she risked her life to try to save this misfortune. So she dressed up as a sweet potato seller, carrying a wooden bucket filled with hot sweet potatoes, and shouted loudly two or three li away from the South Gate: "Selling sweet potatoes!" "Selling sweet potatoes!" After a while, the XXX soldiers arrived. Seeing that there was a sweet potato seller, they rushed to eat them and asked her which road to take to Qingjiangpu. She pointed them to a fork in the road leading to another place. Sure enough, they were fooled. By the time they realized they had been deceived and walked back on this road, the reinforcements had already arrived. So Qingjiangpu was saved. The old woman saw that the goal had been achieved and the wish had been fulfilled, so she returned silently! Later, the people of Qingjiangpu knew about it and said it was the transformation of the Bodhisattva Guanyin, so it has been passed down to this day, and a good story has turned into a myth.

Two Unforgettable Impressions 250

— Yangtze River

Once, I passed in front of the Continental Nanchang on Nanjing Road and saw a well-dressed upper-class man jump out of a rickshaw and walk into the China National Products Company. That person was still very young and a bit frivolous. But he didn't pay the rickshaw fare. The rickshaw puller waited and waited, and became impatient and screamed more anxiously. Naturally, I only had sympathy for him, not dislike, rickshaw pullers are mostly pitiful.

Out of sympathy for him, I stood by, wanting to see the outcome. (Although it was only an insignificant and impractical concern) But after ten minutes, the passenger still hadn't come out. The rickshaw puller had no choice but to pull another customer and leave.

Alas, the so-called upper class!

X X X X

Once again, it was in front of the British barracks in Shanghai. Two anemic Chinese girls were flirting with British soldiers, using fingers to talk and bargain. I knew they were the so-called "saltwater girls."

The price was not settled, and the Chinese girl was about to leave strategically, but her four feet moved very slowly: the British soldier was shouting loudly, probably wanting to change his mind. Many vendors and rickshaw pullers on the roadside were laughing at that situation. Some even said some nasty things. I only had sympathy and a depressed and unhappy heart!

I hope I never see those things again.

Her heart was beating and her face was red. After a long time, she said: This is news. Zhao Weng said: Okay, stop talking, let's talk about serious things, shall we? He said, it's not letting me live in the house for free. There are inevitably some small things in the store, and I would like me to take care of them. I thought it was good, first, I live in the city, I have more friends, and I can find something easy to do every day, so as not to be bored. Secondly, it is not far from the maternity hospital, and Guizhi will be taken care of when she is in confinement. I came back to discuss with you, are you willing or not? When Guizhi heard that she was going to move to the city, she first had a smile on her face. Jiang saw that her father-in-law and daughter-in-law had the same opinion, so naturally she did not disagree. So after discussing for a while, it was decided that they would move into the city three days later. On this day, Zhao Weng first went to the city to arrange the house. Jiang put the furniture to be moved on a large cart and pushed the large cart with Xiaolin all the way. Only Guizhi was a pregnant woman, unable to sit in that heavy cart, so she hired a familiar rickshaw from the street to slowly pull her into the city. (436)

Mother and Daughter 252

— Zhou Junqi

The electric lights in the hotel were so dim and bleak!

K and I were sitting on the edge of the bed chatting idly. Suddenly an old woman walked into the room. Her face, covered with chicken skin-like wrinkles, set off her two lively eyeballs, which made people hate her. Behind her was a girl of about seventeen or eighteen years old with some country habits, standing very naturally outside the threshold.

"Sir, would you like a girl to accompany you..." the old woman said.

Zang Zhi Anwei Shepherd Zang Xi

"..." K and I subconsciously cast a surprised glance at the girl. The old woman then skillfully reached out and dragged the girl to our front.

"Say hello to the gentleman..." the old woman ordered the girl.

"Sir..." The young girl lowered her head to her chest, a blush appeared on her cheeks, and her voice was so soft, so soft.

But we realized that there was something strange about this matter. Obviously, the two of them were not related as mother and daughter, but had another special characteristic, which was exposed from the girl's lowered, shy red face and her pair of melancholy, fearful eyes.

"Is she your mother?" K, who was always impatient and lacked experience in the world, pointed at the old woman and questioned her;

"..." The young girl hesitated for a while, afraid to tell her hidden pain, and barely uttered a "Yes..." from her throat, which seemed to be blocked by something. The voice was very sad, almost crying. Especially the expression on her face was like the pleading expression of a lamb waiting to be slaughtered, which was so touching.

However, the old woman suddenly changed her face and then said fiercely, "Go, go!" The young girl followed the old woman out of the room! Finally disappeared at the end of the corridor.

The electric lights in the hotel were still so dim and bleak

We were lost and silent in the lonely atmosphere!

World News

Tour of Europe 253

— Zhang Ruogu

▲Letter from Berlin (Part 2)

In April weather, night falls quickly in the north. The twilight of Berlin turns into a fairy tale world. The stars in the sky emit timid flashes of light, all of which are ingenious artificial lights.

At night, we can see many strong incandescent lamps in the Berlin metropolis, illuminating various majestic buildings. The parliament, a palace-like building, is immersed in electric light, just like a crystal palace.

Berlin's Parliament

If you live in the city for a long time, you may want to go to the suburbs near Berlin to breathe the fresh air in the forest. The famous "Sanssouci Palace" is the German Versailles. Near the villa, we can mourn the windmill mill called "Sanssouci". According to a German fable passed down from generation to generation, there used to be an old owner living in that mill. The emperor built a villa and imperial garden near the mill. He took a fancy to the mill and wanted the miller to give it to him. Who knew that the old man stubbornly refused. Someone was worried for him, saying that he had offended the emperor and was afraid that he would suffer an unexpected disaster. The old man replied calmly: "The emperor has his own palace and garden, and he can enjoy himself freely. The mill is my property, and I have my rights. If he wants to invade, I can sue him in court. What's there to worry about?" This is the origin of the names "Sanssouci Palace" and "Sanssouci Mill".

If you want other entertainment, you can spend your time in Berlin's major theaters. There are all kinds of operas from the north and south, and you can choose the one that suits your interest and enter. The prices are different, and a seat in front of an orchestra usually costs 20 marks, which is equivalent to 180 square meters of currency. (About 20 yuan in national currency)

This nation, which is rich in practical perseverance and highly modern, is a nation with the soul of a musician. The operas they perform must be seen once. One night, we watched "Der Rosenkavalier", and the music was so beautiful and moving!

If we miss the opportunity to appreciate this musical opera, we will inevitably feel that this trip to Berlin outside the Rhine River is not perfect.

Grain Prices Are Level Due to Rain; Consecutive Days of Rises Show Much Speculation; How to Improve Matters, the Authorities Should Pay Attention 263

There has been no rain in the Yangtze River basin for a long time, and most rivers and streams have dried up. Fields and crops cannot be planted, and those that have been planted have no way to irrigate and can only watch them wither and die. This year's autumn harvest is expected to be poor. However, this concerns the grain situation in the winter of this year and next year, and seems to have little relationship with the current food situation. However, grain merchants and wealthy merchants who have nowhere to use their money are taking advantage of the opportunity to raise grain prices sharply and collect extensively (when new rice entered the market last winter, large merchants and wealthy people believed that rice prices had no hope and were unwilling to hoard them, so rice prices could not be maintained). A speculative fever for grain products has been triggered. Therefore, rice merchants are smiling, while farmers are still frowning. It is important to know that changes in prices cannot escape the laws of supply and demand. The characteristic of Chinese people is to be unprepared in peacetime and panic in times of trouble. Therefore, they are easily used and manipulated by merchants. If the provincial and county governments in the rice-producing areas can truly think about the people's livelihood and cooperate closely to investigate the amount of rice and grain in stock and compile relatively reliable statistics, and then formulate practical and feasible regulatory measures, it is believed that there will not be a severe shortage. However, if it is said but not done, and the market fabricates seemingly true but actually false words, grain prices will rise and fall accordingly. Recently, grain speculation has become increasingly large and has a profound impact on people's livelihood. Those who have relations with foreign rice are taking advantage of it to promote tax-free movements, which has become the most relevant slogan of the times. Observing the stability of the market once foreign rice is secured, it can be seen that the initial panic was purely driven by psychological factors and had nothing to do with the quality of the goods. It is believed that consecutive years of good harvests in the country have both promoted the fall in grain prices and led to the bankruptcy of rural areas, which is difficult to recover. Now, due to a month of drought, the bankruptcy of rural areas has become even more serious. However, the accumulation of grain in various places and the hoarding and speculation of large households are adding to the drought or even rejoicing in misfortune and refusing to release grain. Therefore, the current plan is to first provide relief by selling existing grain at fair prices, and to limit speculative activities. It is important not to see a drought and immediately secure foreign rice without detailed investigation, which would cause more trouble to rural areas.

Flour Market Opening 267

All months showed a uniform downward trend. Foreign wheat was quoted with Chicago down a little 12/100ths and Canada down a little 48/100ths. When the market opened, the weather suddenly turned cool, with overcast skies suggesting that rain might soon be seen in the local area. News that soaking rain had fallen in various locations, including Beijing and Zhenjiang, had eased the anxiety of those who had been worried. Moreover, since the soaring grain prices had prompted the industry to start ordering foreign wheat as a means of emergency relief, it was hoped that the price of rice could gradually be brought down. All of these factors acted like a dose of cooling powder amidst the feverish clamor. Consequently, the opening price was soft, dropping nearly a cent. Later, due to heavy long positions, there was quite a bit of pullback. Many small holders also eagerly sold off their holdings, leading to pervasive selling pressure and declines across all boards. As for spot prices in Tianjin, there was initial excitement, followed by a retreat. "Cannon Cart" was quoted at 4.40 yuan and "Green Boat" at 4.20 yuan. Later telegraphs indicated that prices might continue to fall. As a result, this month's contract fell 2.5 cents, August fell a little 2.5 cents, September and October fell a little 3 cents, November fell a little 3.5 cents, and December fell a little 3 cents.

After the morning opening, the market for all months showed a uniformly declining trend. Foreign wheat quotations showed Chicago and Canada down a little 48/100ths to 12/100ths. This situation was unrelated to the market's ups and downs. The sudden easing of anxiety was because the local area was likely to see rain, Beijing and Zhenjiang had received welcome rain, and there was renewed activity in the market for foreign wheat. Therefore, as soon as the longs were active, the market saw a soft decline. However, this kind of big rise and small pullback was probably not a truly small situation. It would require soaking rain across the drought-stricken areas and genuine orders for wheat to truly suppress the frenzy. Shenbao Local Supplement

Commentary

Preaching to Prisoners in Xuanhua 277

It was reported earlier that the Chinese Buddhist Association sent a letter to Justice Minister Ju Juegong, proposing to send personnel to prisons to preach to prisoners: "Before 1927, prisons in various provinces all had instructors, mostly Buddhist followers... The results were remarkable. Later, due to frequent turmoil, this practice could not be implemented. People are mostly indifferent to Buddhism when they are in good circumstances; they only become aware after suffering setbacks. When someone is imprisoned, the enlightening influence of Buddhism should be applied promptly to help them repent, which is more effective. Even after they are released from prison, they can be good citizens of society. Considering this, the association has already petitioned your office to instruct the courts of all provinces, cities, and counties to allow Buddhist organizations to select and send teachers to prisons to spread Buddhism for enlightenment... If you grant your approval, the benefits to prisoners will be limitless."

Buddhist followers aim to transcend humanity and deliver all living beings. Their divine grace even extends to prisoners in prisons, the gathering place for "evil men" and "rebellious elements," which can only be considered immeasurable merit. We see that Christianity in Western Europe heavily promotes its "ointment that doesn't reach the hand" to many prisoners, sending them to the killing field with a cross, which are all practical expressions of making prisoners "repent." Now, in this time of social unrest and many criminals, the Buddhist Association has come to blow its "dharma conch" again. First, it says that timely enlightenment is more effective, and second, it says that helping them repent can make them good citizens. A heart of helping the world and saving people leaps onto the paper. However, the connection to the path is shallow for the impure, and questions must arise.

First of all, I certainly cannot but admit that if all living beings in the world advocated purity, non-action, and non-competition, the result would naturally be a reduction in worldly evils, and everyone would be a "good citizen of society." However, because human beings are born imperfect due to God's creation, they have the requirements of food, clothing, and shelter and various desires. These things are exclusively occupied by a small number of people. To strive for these things to maintain survival leads to the formation of society as a battlefield of life, producing infinite "evils." If these requirements cannot be obtained properly, the source of "evil" will exist in society one day. If Buddhist followers who are concerned about saving the world want to enlighten them and make them aware, teaching them to tighten their belts, not wear clothes, and lie on the ground may lead them to "repent."

As for the so-called criminals who are mostly indifferent to Buddhism when they are in good circumstances and only become aware after suffering setbacks, they are mostly military men and politicians who have lost power. When they are imprisoned, they may convert to Buddhism. However, once they are free, they will rise again and reorganize their old businesses. Their belief in "great compassion" is only a temporary "hiding" to avoid the storm. It cannot be treated the same as those who are driven to crime by the need for food and clothing after their release from prison. Even if those "desperate" prisoners may become aware and repent due to "timely enlightenment" while imprisoned, they probably cannot solve their real problems by simply following the master's teachings when they are forced by hunger and cold after serving their sentences. At that time, the Buddhist prison instructor's hope for good citizens of society will no longer be "the benefits to prisoners will be limitless."

Originally, religion is a vain and unfounded thing. It not only passively spreads illusions that distance people from reality but also actively compensates for sins and conceals peace. The more unstable society is, the stronger the environment that drives people to "evil" is, and the more it takes this opportunity to spread the seeds of "non-non realms." Passively, it pulls people into a realm of emptiness and vastness. Actively, it tries its best to cover up the source of social evils, blurring the path for people to seek survival, advancement, and social transformation. Therefore, although prisoners in national prisons may repent after being enlightened by Buddhism, they still have the problem of eating and clothing after their release. To make them "good citizens," it is definitely not about converting to Buddhism but about having a real understanding of society and striving for it. Otherwise, the so-called "preaching" is an act of teaching people to repent to Tathagata on an empty stomach.

A Dream 278

— Ling Yu

After rushing around for a day under the scorching sun, I returned home when the lights were on.

"It's cool today, how come you're only back now?" This was my aunt, in whose house I was lodging, asking me.

"Because there was a risk of problems with my job, I went to see my uncle," I answered, exhausted and panting. "It's really cool here today," I said again, sitting on a stool by the windy doorway.

"Today is French Revolution Day, there's a lantern parade; there are also fireworks, a musical band, and all kinds of lanterns in the French Park. It's very lively outside. We went last year." My aunt said to me excitedly.

"I can't go, I need to take a bath and then rest, you guys go," I replied.

The dinner that had been prepared long ago was eaten quickly. My aunt and the five members of her family all tidied themselves up to go see the excitement.

"We'll see something good, don't regret it!" My aunt still wanted to tempt me to go with her as she left.

"I won't regret it," I answered simply.

They left, and the room was quiet, with only me left. The evening breeze was even cooler. I put a rattan chair on the balcony, lay down barefoot and with bare arms, watching the twinkling stars in the sky and listening to the distant sounds of the city. In such a cool and quiet twilight, I felt at ease. Suddenly, as if I couldn't bear the loneliness, I got up, went out, and caught up with my aunt and the others, but they weren't heading towards the French Park. They were walking down a road I had never known before. I asked my aunt in surprise:

"What is this place? Where are you going?"

"Don't you recognize this as XX Road?" 'Where are you going?' you ask even more strangely. Isn't today our country's Revolution Day? XX Association is holding a grand ceremony and a grand celebration. Look, aren't all the people going to participate in this grand event?" My aunt said, pointing to one side with her finger.

Following her finger, I saw a tall building with our country's national flag flying brightly in the wind. A wave of cheers from the people and generous and majestic music came from that side. I was a little confused.

"During the day, weren't all the shops, buses, and a few private cars flying the tricolor flag of red, white, and blue? Why have they all changed to our national flag now?" I murmured softly.

"Are there still tricolor flags? This is our national territory," my aunt said when she heard my words.

"Isn't this the French Concession?" I asked suspiciously.

"You're a complete fool! That was decades ago. Our national territory is our domain. Since that revolution, all the unequal treaties have been abolished, the concessions have been recovered, and the tariffs are autonomous. In short, we occupy the same position as other powerful countries on Earth. For this great revolution, we are commemorating it today with such cheers everywhere," my aunt said proudly.

I thought silently that the things during the day were said to be decades ago, and the memorial day of another country was said to be our memorial day. Why was my aunt lying to me like this today? I asked stutteringly.

"I knew it was French during the day..."

"No need to say it, come with us, you will naturally know when you get there. Do you definitely like to see the memorial day of a foreign country, but don't want to participate in such a great memorial festival of our own!" She said as she walked triumphantly.

I was confused and happy again, and I followed them while involuntarily saying in a voice full of joy: "This is a great memorial day, this is a memorial day worth commemorating!"

"Sleeping here, don't catch a cold," my aunt said softly, pushing my shoulder.

I rubbed my eyes, the starlight was above my head, and the sounds of the city were echoing in the distance. I was still lying in the rattan chair. I dragged my shoes lazily into my room, fell on the bed, but my heart was still beating non-stop, a kind of relief, a kind of joy, and my mouth was still murmuring: "A great memorial day, a memorial day worth commemorating."

Page 18

The Secret of Longevity of the Kerosene King 279

— Feng

John D. Rockefeller, whom many call the "Kerosene King" in America, is one of the world's richest men. The other day was his ninety-fifth birthday. The family celebration was held at his former residence on Lake Lake in New York State. Mr. Rockefeller likes to play golf, and he believes that golf is the secret to longevity.

"Money can't buy a way out of the underworld," although there was this saying in ancient times, Yama, the god of death, will still take some personal feelings into account. People with money will definitely have power. Although this path cannot be bought, "deferred execution" can always be arranged.

Mr. Rockefeller said that golf is the secret to longevity. I dare not believe it. If that were the case, then golf can prolong life and benefit health. Even playing golf on the table can make you live ten or eight years longer. No wonder there are golf injury facilities in several large gardens. Presumably, it is the intention of inviting some old masters, young masters, ladies and young ladies who visit the garden to increase their years.

However, people with money are always broad-minded and content. They always feel comfortable. They can do whatever they like. This is the origin of longevity. If you like sailing, sailing is the secret to longevity. If you like horse racing, horse racing is the secret to longevity. If you like dancing, dancing is also the secret to longevity. If you like gambling, gambling is also the secret to longevity. There are many secrets to longevity for people with money, not just golf.

As long as you have money, living in a loft is like roasting a field frog in such hot weather. You keep complaining, but people with money and power not only live in tall foreign houses but also want to be comfortable and go to famous mountains and scenic spots to escape the summer heat. This kind of body will live at least eight hundred years longer.

The Last Letter 280

— Xue Shu

Qinmei's mother died, not long ago, but when her mother was dying, she was working somewhere. I know very well that she must have been very sad about her mother's death. Why shouldn't she be? She wanted an independent life, she wanted to break free from the shackles of her family, no, more importantly, she wanted to stay away from her hometown to avoid marrying that hooligan-like fiancé. So she struggled in the yarn factory, enduring her gloomy years like a cow or a horse.

I haven't received her letter for almost five months, needless to say, this made me very worried. But a week ago, I received her death letter. Ah! A young girl actually wrote such a letter. Her letter read like this.

...Sister Shan: Do you remember? It has been more than two years since we separated. But, Sister Shan, in these two years, I have suffered all the pain of life in the world. Sister Shan, I used to believe that I could drift like this. But, until now, I deeply feel that all the pain has completely shattered my courage to struggle. Isn't it? A week ago, I still thought so, I always held on to my indomitable ambition to gain light in the dark society, and always looked forward to the day when I would cut down the demons and kill them happily, so I desperately sacrificed everything to move forward, but now everything makes me despair, ah! I recall the pain of the past, sadness and despair, I feel that my heart has been shattered. At this time, my heart hurts as if it is being bitten by a demon, but I have to endure the pain to finish this letter, ah! Sister Shan, I can't help but shed sad tears.

Sister Shan, now I can't bear the pain to move forward anymore, let me tell you: I endured the humiliation and did the hard work in that hellish yarn factory for a year, how fierce and vicious the foreman was, how terrible his face was, he could simply swallow me at any time. From morning to night, I couldn't see the sky, I couldn't see the sun, and there was no moment for you to rest. Sister Shan, my fragile body is naturally inevitable to get sick in such a cruel hell on earth. When I was sick, of course I couldn't go to work anymore, so I had to live in that pigeon cage-like attic for a week. Sister Shan, all my clothes and bedding... have been pawned, but I still haven't paid this month's rent. Sister Shan, it turns out that people's hearts in the world are as black as coal! Seeing that I was so poor and sick, the landlord kicked me out today. At that time, I only knew how to cry sadly, and I didn't know where to go. Suddenly, it seemed that my mother was guiding me in front. Sister Shan, I often saw my mother's dark shadow in the moment of dizziness. So, I turned sorrow into joy, and slowly walked through the bustling place with weak feet and walked to a secluded place, oh! I arrived at my place of rest, and the death-like loneliness was embracing me. Sister Shan, my mother has been waiting for me for a long time. Now I am using a pencil to write this last letter to you under the dim light of the street lamp. If you can receive it, then it will be my greatest wish, because you are the only one in the world who truly understands me. I have to bless you in the dark. Sister Shan, goodbye forever...

Shanghai Has No Summer

"Prostitute Bargain" and "Ruthless" 281

— Yang Yang

Modern commercial operations, due to the shocks of trends, have mostly abandoned their concept of "genuine and unwavering prices." They also deeply understand that advertising and promotion, with their extensive influence, are indeed the strongest weapons in commercial warfare, embodying the idea that "with these to conquer enemies, no enemy cannot be destroyed" and "with these to achieve success, no achievement is unattainable." I remember when my family lived in Tianjin, I often saw shops in both the Chinese and foreign concessions of Tianjin, when they reduced prices to sell goods, some published announcements in newspapers, some distributed leaflets, and some hung various slogans at their doors. The simple slogans that caught the eye and caused surprise were mostly "Hurry up! Big Bargain!" and "Risk it all! Clearing Stock!" We won't discuss whether they were "truly hurrying" or "truly risking it," or whether they were using the old trick of "the wool comes from the sheep." In short, it belongs to competitive business and can be called "bitter operation." Although there are some flashy tricks, as long as the intention is predictable, it seems that commercial ethics have not been lost. Moreover, personal stakes are involved, so how could anyone truly willingly sell at a loss? If that were the case, wouldn't those wealthy merchants have to bring their wives and children, preparing for losses, and wouldn't all the employees of the shop also have to suffer? And why are some department stores opening grandly today, and some limited companies establishing and opening tomorrow? Since they are not fools, throwing capital casually into a void, we can also understand everything!

However, the meanings of advertising slogans like "Hurry up!" and "Risk it all!" are vivid and expressive, truly filled with the local color of Tianjin and worth our appreciation and study.

Recently, I suddenly saw a long rectangular red sign in front of a shop on Stone Road in this city, with two conspicuous black characters: "Prostitute Bargain." This couldn't help but make me suspicious, as it seemed like the northern wind was gradually blowing south, carrying a genuine Tianjin flavor. Could it be that the shop owner is a "Tianjin talker"? However, the word "prostitute" is a taboo in the north, especially when speaking to women. Now this shop is not only "bargaining," but still insists on adding a "prostitute." Although it is speaking to buying and selling goods, to show genuine price reductions and treating customers with sincerity, as if there is nothing more to say. However, if we carefully savor these two characters, "Prostitute Bargain," we suddenly feel a strange interest and can't help but laugh!

Unexpectedly, things in the world often happen in pairs. Yesterday, I suddenly discovered a summer sale advertisement from a Tianjin shop in the Tianjin Dagongbao. It started by placing the two large characters "Ruthless" above the shop's name. I guess the reason for their "ruthlessness" is nothing more than standing on the same front as "Hurry up!" and "Risk it all!" to express their willingness to lose money and promote goods. The wonderful thing is that "Prostitute Bargain" and "Ruthless," from the north and south, echo each other from afar, and I discovered them one after another. A careful appreciation is also a good way to escape the summer heat. Because this kind of thought-provoking article is most likely to make your heart cool!

But there is one thing: if we take a broad view of the dumping policies of Japan and Soviet Russia in their trade with China, they are also "prostitute bargain" and "ruthless," only seeking to sell goods smoothly, regardless of losses. They are of course carrying a political background and implementing their economic invasion, eventually having a day of harvest, which is probably the so-called "fragrant bait to catch golden turtles," luring you to take the bait. Only this kind of "prostitute bargain" can be called truly "ruthless"!

Sincerity Works Miracles 282

— Sanduo

The Panchen Lama met with reporters in Beijing the day before yesterday and expressed the following opinions:

"The south is suffering from severe drought. I sent ten lamas to Qixia Mountain in Nanjing to pray for rain, and as a result, there was heavy rain for two hours. Later, I went to Baohua Mountain to pray for rain, and there was heavy rain for two days."

The Panchen Lama's magic is boundless, and I think his way of praying for rain is just a small part of his skill.

The gentry and merchants of Shanghai saw that there had been no rain for more than twenty days, which led to soaring rice prices and rampant epidemics. Heaven has the virtue of loving life, so they respectfully set up an altar in the Siming Guild Hall to pray for rain. This is different from the Panchen Lama's prayer for rain.

The Panchen Lama relies on Buddhism, so he is so confident. As for the four attendants who died suddenly in the car when the Lama went to Beijing, that was predestined before birth, and Buddhism could not save them. The gentry and merchants of Shanghai relied entirely on a sincere heart to pray for rain, so-called "sincerity works miracles." Sure enough, there was drizzle at noon today (the 17th), although not "heavy," it is also "precious"!

Children 283

— Baishe

They are as lively as little birds, as happy as little birds, shouting and singing like little birds, these innocent and lovely children.

Children are running, jumping, and playing in the garden. I always like to stand at the window of the building behind the garden and watch. The children are focused on playing and don't realize that someone is envying them, which brings a smiling melancholy.

The children's bodies are naturally given to them for activity, never willing to stop for a moment, and the laughter in their mouths never stops. They turn, crawl, and slide from the slide, like a large group of noisy sparrows in the forest in the morning. Although they also cry, their crying does not carry human suffering, only for a small and ridiculous reason. But soon they will be crying and laughing again.

Seeing these children playing unrestrainedly and heartily, I can't help but feel a light feeling in my heart. So I ran downstairs, stepping and jumping, and walked to the middle of the children. The children are not afraid of me, they think I am a companion of the same age as them, and they do not feel uncomfortable because of my joining. My heart feels a burst of joy, because the fact proves that I am still a naughty child, yes, I am still a child, a child.

Since I regard myself as a child, I am willing to do anything that children play. Rolling on the ground, shouting, somersaulting, everything is the same as the children, but the only difference from the children is that I know it myself. Because every time I jump, I feel that my legs are stiff. Although things that children do without effort, I feel heavy, my joints are clumsy, and my posture is unnatural. But since the children do not regard me as someone other than a child, and I still retain a little of the child's component, this point seems to be quite comforting.

"Good child, give me a kiss." The child does not need to worry, puts two bright red little lips close to my mouth, leaving a moist imprint, but he looks at the short mustache on my lips with round and large black eyes. So, I am sad, I know that this stinging thing has made the child's tender skin feel uncomfortable.

The sun is down, the children tear, shout, and scream, as if a large group of small birds have flown away, they jump and laugh. They did not invite me to go with them. So I stayed alone in the garden, coldly, jump, my legs are so clumsy, sing, what to sing? I touched the short mustache on my lips with one hand and pondered alone. Clearly the children have abandoned me, pray to heaven, can you turn me back ten years?

Yes, I have been away from the children for ten years.

Novel

Revenge (3) 284

— Translated by Hungarian Yuri Bakirojia

A man stood in the center of the house. His face was painful and desperate. One hand held a letter, the other a repeating pistol. He was so deeply immersed in his grief that he did not notice that someone was standing behind him.

He raised the hand with the pistol, and in that instant, he was affectionately embraced—a pair of white arms. He suddenly turned his head.

"You? Alice, is that you?"

"Yes, it's me!"

This sudden surprise stopped his mouth. The girl took the pistol from his hand with a sad smile and threw it on the table.

After a long silence, the man spoke.

"Why did you come?"

"Because I love you."

"I don't understand... You love me, but tomorrow you are going to marry another man."

"Because I should... Because they forced me... My father's life depends on all this..."

"Then why did you come?"

The girl said lowly, holding the repeating pistol:

"I foresaw this."

"Then, you came to stop me... Alice!"

The girl stammered almost awkwardly:

"No... Just for this... I came..."

"But...?"

Her forehead blushed.

"Can't you guess?"

"No. I haven't thought of..."

The girl ran over and hid her purple face on the man's chest, whispering only what his ear could hear:

"I am willing... I am willing to be... Yours..."

Film Special

The Audience's Ostrich Policy and the Masks Worn by Stars (Part 2) 285

— Suyin

By now, a film actor has reached the point where they cannot tell the truth and have to lie. Telling the truth in a down-to-earth manner is too ordinary for the audience. They must follow the audience's psychology, say what they like to hear, and what they like to hear is nothing more than empty, romantic stories. The reason why the American boxing king Cunnington is not popular with the public, although his name is known to all women and children in the country, is because he is too honest and not romantic enough. He is too loyal to the audience, and he does not know how to deceive them a little to please them. He often tells people: "The reason why I want to box with people is entirely for money. When I have money, I will not box, but stay at home comfortably drinking hot milk and reading Shakespeare." Alas, for the sake of money! Drinking milk? Reading Shakespeare! That is so lacking in romantic flavor! If he said, "I am for fame! When I succeed, I will travel around the world and compete with the strong men of various countries!" Or say, "I am going to England to teach the Prince of Wales to box!" Then everyone would applaud thunderously.

Raymond Navarro is a very kind person. You can invite him to drink, and he can drink cup after cup without refusing. He also likes to be sociable and have fun. If you invite him to a banquet, wherever there are sweet women and soft music, he will be there. And before the night is over, he must sing a "Sweet Antriline" or play a piece on the piano to be considered a complete evening. Raymond has many ways to entertain, but what is circulated among the "people" is only one kind of his "good at singing." Everything else is not convenient to say, and dare not say, why say things that offend the public? It is even more unnecessary to say that some people publicize him like a missionary, saying that he likes to sing hymns, etc., praising him as if he were a white dove among a group of crows. The same is true for Joan Crawford. If you are not afraid of being scolded, you can say that Joan likes to go out at night: she often dances and seeks pleasure outside all night long; she likes to dance Charleston and all kinds of romantic and unrestrained behaviors. Because what the public knows is that Joan Crawford is a person with "ambition greater than everything else"! She works hard all day long; she overcomes all difficulties; she is a person who is always fighting with the environment!

There is also a person who is "always fighting with the environment," that is, Jean Harlow. The newspapers have publicized her as if she were the most unfortunate person in the world, so thousands of viewers shed tears of sympathy for her. Her first husband was too young; her second husband was too old. They died, committed suicide, leaving a pitiful little widow, and she is still struggling hard! Yes, she is the bravest woman ever. If you say something else, you have to be careful that people who are superstitious about Harlow hear you!

The love triangles that have occurred in Hollywood, not to say that the world has never seen, even the residents of Hollywood are almost speechless. The triangle between Chaderton, Brent, and Debs made people dizzy and unable to approach. Ruth Chaderton divorced Ralph Forbes and married George Brent; but Ruth still kept in constant contact with Ralph. Recently, Ruth is going to divorce George again and return to Ralph. How do you think a husband should be, how should a good friend be, how should a friend also be a husband, how should a husband become a friend? Can this problem be solved in trigonometry? But everyone knows that Ruth Chaderton is a highly educated and morally noble person. They don't even know that she likes to chew gum, and they don't want to know.

In Lincoln's time, the United States did not have movies. At that time, people's hearts may have been different from now. Worshiping hypocrisy, escaping reality, and not wanting to know the real situation, willing to comfort oneself with falsehood, these are all characteristics of modern people, which Lincoln did not anticipate. (The end)

Film Review

Review of "Dragon Horse Swordsman" 286

— Ling He

Flaming Guns 丨 New Light

Probably people who often watch American movies all know that there is a horse called Tony and a person called Tom Mix. He and it often rush back and forth on the screen. Now Tony is dead, and all that is left is Tom Mix. However, he has no opponent, so he found another horse and named it Little Tony. It appeared in "Dragon Horse Swordsman."

However, we are really tired of watching this kind of play.

Western filmmakers have long had a model. Every Western film just needs to be taken out of this stereotype, which is very convenient. However, because of this, we are really tired of watching it. It is always the same set of things.

The old story, the old directing techniques, almost do not need to be re-examined. Anyway, it is just this kind of thing.

Like this kind of Western film, it should not exist now.

But some people say that Western films are only for the little people to vent their anger. The reason is that the overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, because they have suffered various oppressions, like to watch these films. So we (referring to we intellectuals) do not need to demand the correct "consciousness" of the works, anyway, it is just for the "little people" to watch. However, this point is not something we dare to agree with. Precisely because Western films are welcomed by the general audience with low intellectual standards, precisely because the scenes of fighting and excitement suit their tastes, precisely because Western films are close to their lives, so we demand the authors of Western films even more urgently, there must be correct content in them, and then they can become film works that are beneficial to the "little people."

Moreover, when we criticize a film work, we never stand only on the position of our few people. On the contrary, our demands must become the demands of the general audience. Do you mean to say that we audience should exclude the "little people"? To say it again, our opinions are the opinions of the general audience.

Why shouldn't Western films have new content? Assuming that the unique film form has to continue to exist. For example, what is popular now is heroes and good men, eliminating violence and bringing peace, and finally marrying beauties to end, then we can also attack individual heroism, make the oppressed masses fight for justice, eliminate hooligans and gangsters, and even eliminate corrupt officials. There can also be fighting scenes, and there can also be riding horses and galloping. Why can't it be welcomed by the general "little people" audience?

We are not against the form of Western films, but we have to demand new content. This is our conclusion.

A scene from "Gold Rush" starring John Bowers丨Great Shanghai Screening 287

Chinese Music and Film 288

— Mo Shuai

"Sculpture," "painting," and "music" are, strictly speaking, the main tools for promoting the "cultural juggernaut." These arts can give "humanity" great benefits in indirect and direct ways.

Speaking of the above few, the most backward in China is of course "music." Whether it is folk or stage, what is played is only some extremely monotonous "melodies." The dull "rhythm" that has remained unchanged for thousands of years is forever pressing down on the talented, with no day to raise their heads!

"Instrumental music" is also very simple and crude in China. What about "vocal music"? A man with a naturally thick vocal cord insists on singing Qingyi Huashan with a sharp voice; conversely, a woman breaks her throat to sing Da Hualian. Although my country's "Peking Opera" studies "diction," "intonation," "rhythm," and "beat," etc., and the West pays attention to "scales," "tempo," "dynamics," "beats," etc. in "singing," which are equally important; but without reality, it will not be able to move forward and lose the original effect and value of "music" and "life," isn't this drawback undeniable?

Since the infiltration of Westernization into the East, there has been considerable construction in singing; unfortunately, like a child with congenital deficiencies and a lack of growth ability, it has always been in its infancy, wasting its youth!

But my country's film has made special speed progress. Under the strict supervision of general critics, it is galloping forward like a fly. In the process of repeated changes, it has swallowed up the considerable power of the old drama, it has penetrated into the people, and it is almost about to rush into the ranks of world-famous films. Why can "Lullaby," "Come Back," and the recent "Fisherman's Song" become popular among the people in a short time? It is because it is a "movie song."

"Film" itself needs "music," and "music" can be spread through "film." Then the relationship between "music" and film is self-evident. At the same time, a heavy burden has been placed on the shoulders of those engaged in film.

In the past sound films, we have seen "Erhuang" and "Xipi" that have been moved from the stage to the screen, and "scandalous songs" that are equally popular among the people. But these are all undesirable old things.

The recent "Fisherman's Song" has changed its style, (such as the two sentences "fish are difficult to catch and boat rent is heavy, fishermen are poor for generations") which can truly grasp the center of consciousness and make the audience have infinite feelings. The words are also simple and easy to understand: but the "melody" is not very beautiful, but it is much better than other songs.

In addition, how should we build a new path for "film music"? Now, due to space limitations, we cannot discuss it in detail.

Film Novel

Princess Thirty Days (Thirty-Day Princess) (6) 289

— Jin Que

Duke Nicholas was a simple-minded person. After hearing Gilke's words, he took Gilke to search Katherine's room in Glashin Building. In this search, Gilke found a book in the back of a drawer. He opened it and saw that it was nothing else but Naixue's notebook. This further proved that Princess Katherine was impersonated by Naixue, and York was even more ecstatic to get this true evidence. Nicholas was almost going crazy, but not as ecstatic as Gilke. He felt that this matter was very suspicious. He was also worried about the real Katherine. So he felt that he had to notify King Toronia. He made a long-distance call to the king. But Nicholas was a person with loose lips. Gilke, in order to prevent him from leaking the news and keep his secret, accompanied him east and west every day.

The trip of Wang Bao and others was scheduled for ten days. When they came back, the real Princess Katherine had recovered from her illness. The place where she lived was another floor in Glashin Building. The real princess then invited the fake princess to come and meet her. When Princess Catalina and Naixue met, the two looked at each other and found it difficult to distinguish each other, so they became very close to each other. The two of them rested together. One was called Xuexue, and the other was Naixue. The two of them eliminated the distinction between superior and inferior and directly addressed each other by their nicknames. Xuexue asked: "Have you seen Nicholas?" Naixue said with a sympathetic look, as if it was a pity that a fresh flower was inserted in a pile of dung, and told the princess everything about Madison and Bode. She also said: "Madison is a very good person. But Glashin hates him very much in his heart. Therefore, when the last dance party is held tomorrow night, I want to avenge him and send him a fake Baoxing··Send it to him··" Xuexue said: "Tomorrow night, I will participate in the last dance party myself." She also smiled mischievously and said: "Whether the treasure is a raw treasure star or not, I will arrange it. Naixue, okay?" Naixue agreed happily. Hua··Da··Da··Da··" The long trumpet was blowing. Princess Catalina. Theodoras. Maglita walked out gracefully and walked lightly to the end of the large ballroom to sit on the throne. She returned to Yiyan and said: "Before we say goodbye, we would like to express our gratitude to two great American people, one is Luculus. Mr. Glashin; and the other is Bode, Mr. Madison. We now respectfully present the highest honor Baoxing of our country to these two gentlemen." When the two gentlemen heard this, they immediately walked to the front of the princess. An attendant stood upright on the side, holding a brocade mat containing two Baoxing, one was a real Baoxing, and the other was an Iron Cross. Princess Catalina first took an Iron Cross and was about to pin it on for Glashin. Glashin hurriedly shouted in a low voice: "No, no··That one, that one··" He was still thinking that the princess was Naixue. But the princess ignored him and pinned a cross on him. The handsome young Bode, Madison, actually safely got a real Baoxing. (To be continued)
